# *lad* *services* <_num_> *thousand citizens* *annually*.
# *lad* *services* <more than _high_> *thousand citizens* *annually*.
# contradiction
# *lad*: lad; the dmv; mcdonalds; our church; 
# *services*: services; refuses; kills; litigates; 
# *thousand citizens*: thousand citizens; animals; dogs; claims; 
# *annually*: annually; right now; with ease; simultaneously; 

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = services>>  <<*thousand citizens* = thousand citizens>>  <<*annually* = annually>> 
lad services 39 thousand citizens annually.
lad services more than 49 thousand citizens annually.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = services>>  <<*thousand citizens* = dogs>>  <<*annually* = right now>> 
lad services 46 dogs right now.
lad services more than 47 dogs right now.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = services>>  <<*thousand citizens* = dogs>>  <<*annually* = simultaneously>> 
lad services 41 dogs simultaneously.
lad services more than 43 dogs simultaneously.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = services>>  <<*thousand citizens* = claims>>  <<*annually* = annually>> 
lad services 36 claims annually.
lad services more than 39 claims annually.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = refuses>>  <<*thousand citizens* = thousand citizens>>  <<*annually* = annually>> 
lad refuses 42 thousand citizens annually.
lad refuses more than 45 thousand citizens annually.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = refuses>>  <<*thousand citizens* = animals>>  <<*annually* = with ease>> 
lad refuses 42 animals with ease.
lad refuses more than 47 animals with ease.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = refuses>>  <<*thousand citizens* = claims>>  <<*annually* = with ease>> 
lad refuses 43 claims with ease.
lad refuses more than 46 claims with ease.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = refuses>>  <<*thousand citizens* = claims>>  <<*annually* = simultaneously>> 
lad refuses 34 claims simultaneously.
lad refuses more than 39 claims simultaneously.
contradiction

# args:  <<*lad* = lad>>  <<*services* = kills>>  <<*thousand citizens* = thousand citizens>>  <<*annually* = annually>>

contradiction
